Let's make a game!
  name:Wall Destroyer
  by:Tellurium
  created:04/21/2014
  updated:11/10/2024
  version:2.3.5

Settings
  building cost increase:110%
  building cost refund:75%
  stylesheet:https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Qjuh/walldestroyer/refs/head/main/walldestroyer.css

Layout
  *main
    contains:clickables, resources

  *clickables
    contains:Buttons

  *resources
    contains:Resources
    header:Resources
  
  *stats
    contains:Achievements
    header:Achievements
   
  *store
    contains:upgrades, buildings
  
  *buildings
    contains:BulkDisplay, Buildings
  
  *upgrades
    contains:Upgrades
    header:Upgrades

  *log
    contains:Log

Buttons
  *hitWall
  on click:
    gain 1 money
    gain 1 totalMoney
    gain 1 handDamage
  end
  shown
  name:Punch wall
  tag:clickable
  icon:http://i.imgur.com/108BtPH.png

  *makeBricks
  on click:
    gain 1 bricks
    gain 1 totalBricks
    gain 1 handBricks
  end
  name:Create Bricks
  tag:clickable
  icon:http://i.imgur.com/Tdh80P1.png
  hidden

  *reset
  on click:
    $prestige = prePrestige
    gain $prestige prestige
    $won = goldBricks
    gain $won timesWon
    $bonus = bonusBossBrick
    gain $bonus bonusBossPoint
    $space = spaceBossBrick
    gain $space spaceBossPoint
    $time = timeBossBrick
    gain $time timeBossPoint
    $end = endBossBrick
    gain $end endBossPoint
    $win = winBricks
    gain $win timesActuallyWon
    gain 1 resetTimes
    lose resetUnlock
    lose finalWallUnlock
    hide lastBuilding
    $walls = wallsDestroyed
    gain $walls totalWalls
    lose tag:loseonreset
    show destroyWall
    log Time Rewound: Your cosmic knowledge has been converted into future knowledge capsules.
    toast The Time Bear is coming.
  end
  name:Rewind time (Removes all buildings & resources, converts cosmic knowledge into prestige)
  req:have resetUnlock
  
  *damageConverter
  on click:
    $prestige = totalMoney * 0.0000000000000000000000000000000005
    gain $prestige prePrestige
    lose totalMoney
  end
  name:Convert all damage to cosmic knowledge
  req:have damageConvUnlock

Buildings

  *timeCounter
  on tick:
    if (resetTimes >= 1) gain 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timeSinceReset
    gain 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timePlayed
  end
  always hidden
  start with:1

  *destroyWall
  desc:"Destroy the wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>25</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>250,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
  cost:1000000000000 totalMoney, 1 wallRequirement
  on earn:
    gain 250000000000 money
    gain 25 bricks
    gain 25 totalBricks
    gain 1 wallsDestroyed
    gain 1 prePrestige
    gain 1 wallRequirement
    hide this
    show wallMultiplier
  end
  name:Destroy wall
  tag:loseonreset
  shown
  *destroyBigWall
  desc:"Destroy the big 2nd wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>100</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>25,000,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
  cost:100000000000000 totalMoney, 1 wallRequirement
  on earn:
    gain 25000000000000 money
    gain 100 bricks
    gain 100 totalBricks
    gain 1 wallsDestroyed
    gain 1 prePrestige
    gain 1 wallRequirement
    hide this
    show magicLevel2
    show giantUnlock
  end
  name:Destroy 2nd wall
  req:1 destroyWall
  tag:loseonreset
  *destroyHugeWall
  desc:"Destroy the huge 3rd wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>10,000</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>2,500,000,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
